<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Transcribed, edited (by John Caldwell) and published in 2011 by Stainer &amp; Bell. (Parts published by Denis Stevens in 1951, 1954 &amp; 1973, in Musica Britannica I.) See e.g. <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/oclc/701796816">WorldCat</a></span>.)
</p>
